I have always dabbled in freelancing but it wasn't until a few years ago I really only did just that...contract to contract. Each year during tax time I found myself sifting through receipts and countless transaction lists and STILL owing almost as much as the deductions I thought I would get.

So, after paying and paying I finally Googled "best freelancer bookkeeping tools" and Keeper Tax popped up. It was then that I tried it out for 30 days and quickly saw the benefits- from the texts confirming potential write offs, automatically sorting my expenses while eliminating the dreaded never-ending lists, boxes of receipts and keeping a separate spreadsheet...then learning they could do my taxes for free or a nominal fee was even better...then the rolled out the feature of calculating quarterly taxes and all of this for only <$10/month. Hell yeah! I'd be a fool not to.

The best thing about Keeper Tax is that when you receive the texts about potential write-offs and you respond...it's a REAL person...not a bot. I've sent happy faces and received them back. LOL. Super simple but knowing that a REAL person is communicating with you is the best.<//text>

* The freshly squeezed juices are soooo good! Very refreshing, although not cheap (~$6-7 for a medium sized glass)
* The food is fresh and good - Chocolate chip pancakes were delicious!

The bad
* PSA! The tip is already included when you get the check! - They never mentioned that, and I found out about it a few hours too late. I know it's my fault as you should scan the bill and verify, but that usually happens when there is a big party - We were four people, and no one mentioned anything about it. Really annoying and makes you feel cheated.
* The place is tiny but we were ready for that and joined the queue from home via Yelp. When we came, we were the third party in line (total of four people). With all that, we've waited over 50 minutes to be seated. Not sure if we got unlucky, but this something you need to take into consideration
* Brunch - The potatoes were good, a bit too salty, the eggs were great, but no salt or pepper at all.  Kind of weird.

Due to the issue with the tip, while the place is nice, I feel like it is not entirely honest and I won't be coming back.< /review>< Pictures>

<review>Wait: As there are very few brunch spots around the Inner Richmond, this place tends to have a 20-30 min wait. They do have the Yelp reservation system though, so you can reserve your spot in line ahead of time without having to actually wait outside.

Ambiance: The place is pretty small, but has a cozy feel. Even though it's usually busy, service is pretty fast and staff is friendly and attentive.

Food: I had the Crazy Moco with a side of bacon. The pork katsu was slightly dry, but the crust was super crispy. The gravy was very rich and had a nice little kick (though I could use a little more). The bacon was nice and thick, but still crispy. My companion had the crab Benedict. The eggs were poached well and the hollandaise was nice and creamy. The crab wasn't too sweet, but was still good.

Price: The portions are quite big here, but the price seemed a bit too high for what you are getting. The Benedict dish ended up being around $30.</review>< GmapID>

< text>
We've been taking our two dogs to the Lake Forest location for years. They've also been at the San Clemente location  a couple of times. Our dogs don't do the playgroup because they don't always play nice with strange dogs. However, what I love about Paws is that there's a separate room where a staff member will take dogs to play that don't do the larger group. They also go on numerous walks and runs. A staff member once told me one of my dogs was their best skateboarder dog! I never feel they don't get enough attention or exercise, despite not doing playgroup. And they've never come home sick (dogs are required to get the bordetalla vaccine every six months to be allowed to stay there.) We tried a number of other facilities before Paws, and none of them could come close to the care and attention Paws gives to our dogs. I also love the work they do with rescue dogs.< /text>

<Rate>5<//Rate><Review>A glimpse into the commercial past. This was a passion of an avid collector. This pre WW2 exhibit of general merchandise available in a common US general store is extensive: from bulk food containers to articles of clothing and a complete Great Depression era pharmacy -- everything is authentic right down to the 80+ year old pickles in an oak barrel (we were kindly offered to try one but we politely refused). For less than a dollar for admission you can see some recognizable favorites and bygone novelties of a less techy yesteryear.< /Review><Pics>None< /Pics><Response>None<//Response><GmapID>0x80db1ba5d791f05f:0xe3bced58edcee51c<//GmapID></record></dataset><record>

<userid>109248964881428796702<//userid><user_name>Casey Wilson<//user_name><Date>1567290506820<//Date><Rate>3< /Rate>< text>
I hate to only leave 3 stars, because the employees are nice enough (not overly friendly, but they get the job done) and the sandwich is tasty, but good grief, it's 11 or 12 bucks and it's so small!
I really really wanted to like this place. It's a 5 minute walk to get here, it's locally owned (I think) and it has great reviews. But if I take a 5 minute drive to forklift, I get just as friendly employees and twice the sandwich for the same price and the wait is nowhere nearly as long.
Which leads me to my next point, the wait.
I'm not sure why it takes so long, but plan on at least 10 minutes after ordering, but probably longer. I've been twice now, and as much as it pains me, I probably won't be coming back for the sandwiches.

To the owner who responded:
So I *have* to give you a 5 star review because you think my hard earned money (which matters less than your hard earned money apparently) doesn't afford me an opinion? I'm glad you clearly have a devoted following, and I'm glad they love you. I'm not your target demographic and neither is everyone else, so I can't leave a review that shares things that are important to me because your bread is more important?
I'm not going to let you bully me in to giving a different review like I see you trying to do to other customers.< /text>
